"The Venetian Macao (Chinese: Êæ≥ÈñÄÂ®ÅÂ∞ºÊñØ‰∫∫Â∫¶ÂÅáÊùëÈÖíÂ∫ó) is a luxury hotel and casino resort in Macau, China, owned by Las Vegas Sands. The Venetian is a 39-story,[1] $2.4 billion anchor for the seven hotels on the Cotai Strip in Macau. The 10,500,000-square-foot (980,000 m2) Venetian Macao is modeled on its sister casino resort The Venetian Las Vegas, and is the seventh-largest building in the world by floor area. The Venetian Macao is the largest casino in the world, and the largest single structure hotel building in Asia."
